         * fall back to the stdlib where they aren't provided and fail at
         * build/link time. In case the user provides a header, including

        #endif

            #if !__has_builtin(__builtin_sched_getcpu)
                #error "__builtin_sched_getcpu not found"
            #endif
        #elif ! defined(sched_getcpu)
            __builtin_sched_getcpu;
        #endif
        return 0;
        }

Code:
 
        int main(void) {

        /* With some toolchains (MSYS2/mingw for example) the compiler
         * provides various builtins which are not really implemented and
         * fall back to the stdlib where they aren't provided and fail at
         * build/link time. In case the user provides a header, including
         * the header didn't lead to the function being defined, and the
         * function we are checking isn't a builtin itself we assume the
         * builtin is not functional and we just error out. */
        #if !1 && !defined(htonll) && !0
            #error "No definition for __builtin_htonll found in the prefix"
        #endif

        #ifdef __has_builtin
            #if !__has_builtin(__builtin_htonll)
                #error "__builtin_htonll not found"
            #endif
        #elif ! defined(htonll)
            __builtin_htonll;
        #endif
        return 0;
        }

  #ifndef _GNU_SOURCE
  #define _GNU_SOURCE
  #endif

  #include <stddef.h>
  #include <sys/types.h>

  #include <string.h>
  #include <limits.h>
  /* Put unistd.h before time.h as that triggers localtime_r/gmtime_r
   * function availability on recentish Mingw-w64 platforms. */
  #include <unistd.h>
  #include <time.h>
  #include <errno.h>
  #include <fcntl.h>

  #include <pthread.h>

  static void *f(void *p) { return NULL; }
  int main(void)
  {
    int setsize = CPU_ALLOC_SIZE(64);
    pthread_t thread;
    cpu_set_t *cpuset;
    pthread_create(&thread, 0, f, 0);
    cpuset = CPU_ALLOC(64);
    CPU_ZERO_S(setsize, cpuset);
    pthread_setaffinity_np(thread, setsize, cpuset);
    pthread_getaffinity_np(thread, setsize, cpuset);
    CPU_FREE(cpuset);
    return 0;
  }
